21-23 Point Modern Decklists
============================



 Posted in **Event Coverage**
 on February 3, 2018 






![](https://media.magic.wizards.com/styles/auth_small/public/images/person/authorpic_EventCoverageStaff.jpg)
By Event Coverage Staff











 


One player finished with 23 points (7-1-2) in the Modern portion of Pro Tour *Rivals of Ixalan*, 5 players earned 22 points (7-2-1), and 38 player reached 21 (7-3) points.


23 points (7-1-2)
=================
